help 2022-09-29 14:31:28 Ask other people that has made ships (preferably people that has made a ship from the Nimitz class) and ask them for any tips or how did they make their ship. Finally, you can have years of practice, remake/remaster your designated ship after making it.
I’ve used all of the tactics like asking others how to be better, looking at footage and remaking and incorporating the feedback from my first attempt.
In conclusion, making anything in Plane Crazy and is willing to improve is just like making an essay
